# Pinterest SEO Checklist

Generated from the current Next.js App Router SEO data sources: `src/app/sitemap.ts`, `src/lib/programmatic/*`, and `src/lib/data/*`. This checklist intentionally does not create images, publish pins, or modify SEO pages.

## Summary

- Total SEO pages found: 155
- Total recommended pins: 652
- Minimum pins to create: 310
- Stretch pins to create: 775
- High priority pages: 103
- Medium priority pages: 33
- Low priority pages: 19
- Pages to treat first: [Best Asia Trips from Vancouver Under $3,500](/compare/best-asia-trips-from-vancouver-under-3500); [Best Europe Trips from Toronto Under $3,000](/compare/best-europe-trips-from-toronto-under-3000); [Best Warm Destinations from Toronto Under $2,500](/compare/best-warm-destinations-from-toronto-under-2500); [Japan vs South Korea Travel Cost](/compare/japan-vs-south-korea-travel-cost); [Mexico vs Colombia from Montreal](/compare/mexico-vs-colombia-from-montreal); [Portugal vs Spain Travel Budget](/compare/portugal-vs-spain-travel-budget); [Bali, Indonesia Travel Budget Guide](/destinations/bali); [Bangkok, Thailand Travel Budget Guide](/destinations/bangkok); [Barcelona, Spain Travel Budget Guide](/destinations/barcelona); [Cancun, Mexico Travel Budget Guide](/destinations/cancun)

## Status Legend

- `[ ] Not started`
- `[~] In progress`
- `[x] Done`
- `[!] Needs update`

## Recommended Production Rule

- Minimum: 2 different Pinterest pins per SEO page
- Ideal: 3 to 5 different Pinterest pins per SEO page
- High priority: 5 pins
- Medium priority: 3 pins
- Low priority: 2 pins

## Weekly Pinterest Plan

- Day 1: High priority origin/budget and comparison pages.
- Day 2: High priority destination and budget-travel pages.
- Day 3: Medium priority itinerary and destination guide pages.
- Day 4: Medium priority guide and destination pages.
- Day 5: Remaining low priority pages.
- Day 6: Variations and tests for titles, overlays, and cost breakdown formats.
- Day 7: Audit published pins, update statuses, add Pinterest URLs, and flag pages that need new variants.

## Pages Excluded Or Ambiguous

- Legacy travel cost duration pages excluded for the same reason: 195 URLs, e.g. `/travel-cost/japan/7-days`, `/travel-cost/japan/10-days`, `/travel-cost/japan/14-days`, `/travel-cost/portugal/7-days`, `/travel-cost/portugal/10-days`.
- If those legacy routes become indexable later, add them to the checklist with 2 pins minimum each, or regenerate this document from the same data sources.
